	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">First Sino-Japanese War</h1>
	
	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>
		
		
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>
		<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r904532608">@media all and (min-width:720px){.mw-parser-output .desktop-float-right{box-sizing:border-box;float:right;clear:right}}</style><div class="mw-stack desktop-float-right"><div style="overflow:hidden;margin:1px"><table class="infobox vevent" style="width:25.5em;border-spacing:2px;"><tbody><tr><th class="summary" colspan="2" style="background-color:#C3D6EF;text-align:center;vertical-align:middle;font-size:110%;">First Sino-Japanese War</th></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;border-bottom:1px solid #aaa;line-height:1.5em;"><a href="/wiki/File:First_Sino-Japanese_War.svg" class="image" title="First Sino-Japanese War, major battles and troop movements"><img alt="First Sino-Japanese War, major battles and troop movements" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/First_Sino-Japanese_War.svg/300px-First_Sino-Japanese_War.svg.png" decoding="async" width="300" height="392" War, major battles and troop movements</td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><table style="width:100%;margin:0;padding:0;border:0"><tbody><tr><th style="padding-right:1em">Date</th><td>25 July 1894&#160;– 17 April 1895<br />(8&#160;months, 2&#160;weeks and 2&#160;days)</td></tr><tr><th style="padding-right:1em">Location</th><td><div class="location"><a href="/wiki/Korean_Peninsula" title="Korean Peninsula">Korea</a>, <a href="/wiki/Manchuria" title="Manchuria">Manchuria</a>, <a href="/wiki/Formosa" class="mw-redirect" title="Formosa">Taiwan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Yellow_Sea" title="Yellow Sea">Yellow Sea</a></div></td></tr><tr><th style="padding-right:1em">Result</th><td>
<p>Japanese victory
</p>
<ul><li>Significant loss of prestige for the Qing Empire</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Joseon" title="Joseon">Joseon</a> removed from the Qing Empire's vassalage</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Korean_Peninsula" title="Korean Peninsula">Korean Peninsula</a> transferred to Japanese <a href="/wiki/Sphere_of_influence" title="Sphere of influence">sphere of influence</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Shimonoseki" title="Treaty of Shimonoseki">Treaty of Shimonoseki</a></li></ul></td></tr><tr><th style="padding-right:1em">Territorial<br />changes</th><td>
The <a href="/wiki/Qing_dynasty" title="Qing dynasty">Qing Empire</a> cedes <a href="/wiki/Taiwan_under_Qing_rule" title="Taiwan under Qing rule">Taiwan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Penghu" title="Penghu">Penghu</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Liaodong_Peninsula" title="Liaodong Peninsula">Liaodong Peninsula</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Empire_of_Japan" title="Empire of Japan">Empire of Japan</a>.</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="background-color:#C3D6EF;text-align:center;vertical-align:middle;font-size:110%;">Belligerents</th></tr><tr><td style="width:50%;border-right:1px dotted #aaa;">
<b><span class="datasortkey" data-sort-value="China"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b6/Flag_of_China_%281889%E2%80%931912%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_China_%281889%E2%80%931912%29.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b6/Flag_of_China_%281889%E2%80%931912%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_China_%281889%E2%80%931912%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b6/Flag_of_China_%281889%E2%80%931912%29.svg/45px-Flag_of_China_%281889%E2%80%931912%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="750" data-file-height="500" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Qing_dynasty" title="Qing dynasty">China</a></span></b></td><td style="width:50%;padding-left:0.25em">
<b><span class="datasortkey" data-sort-value="Japan"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Flag_of_Japan_%281870%E2%80%931999%29.svg/22px-Flag_of_Japan_%281870%E2%80%931999%29.svg.png" decoding="async" width="22" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Flag_of_Japan_%281870%E2%80%931999%29.svg/33px-Flag_of_Japan_%281870%E2%80%931999%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Flag_of_Japan_%281870%E2%80%931999%29.svg/43px-Flag_of_Japan_%281870%E2%80%931999%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="700" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Empire_of_Japan" title="Empire of Japan">Japan</a></span></b></td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="background-color:#C3D6EF;text-align:center;vertical-align:middle;font-size:110%;">Commanders and leaders</th></tr><tr><td style="width:50%;border-right:1px dotted #aaa;">
<b><a href="/wiki/Guangxu_Emperor" title="Guangxu Emperor">Guangxu Emperor</a></b><br /><span class="nowrap"><a href="/wiki/Empress_Dowager_Cixi" title="Empress Dowager Cixi">Empress Dowager Cixi</a></span><br /><a href="/wiki/Li_Hongzhang" title="Li Hongzhang">Li Hongzhang</a><br /><a href="/wiki/Liu_Kunyi" title="Liu Kunyi">Liu Kunyi</a><br /><a href="/wiki/Song_Qing_(Qing_dynasty)" title="Song Qing (Qing dynasty)">Song Qing</a><br /><a href="/wiki/Ding_Ruchang" title="Ding Ruchang">Ding Ruchang</a>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Killed_in_action" title="Killed in action"><span style="font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,&#39;Old English Text MT&#39;,serif"><b>&#8224;</b></span></a><br /><a href="/wiki/Liu_Buchan" title="Liu Buchan">Liu Buchan</a>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Killed_in_action" title="Killed in action"><span style="font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,&#39;Old English Text MT&#39;,serif"><b>&#8224;</b></span></a><br /><a href="/wiki/Ye_Zhichao" title="Ye Zhichao">Ye Zhichao</a><br /><a href="/wiki/Zuo_Baogui" title="Zuo Baogui">Zuo Baogui</a>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Killed_in_action" title="Killed in action"><span style="font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,&#39;Old English Text MT&#39;,serif"><b>&#8224;</b></span></a></td><td style="width:50%;padding-left:0.25em">
<b><a href="/wiki/Emperor_Meiji" title="Emperor Meiji">Meiji Emperor</a></b><br /><a href="/wiki/It%C5%8D_Hirobumi" title="Itō Hirobumi">Itō Hirobumi</a><br /><a href="/wiki/Yamagata_Aritomo" title="Yamagata Aritomo">Yamagata Aritomo</a><br /><a href="/wiki/Nozu_Michitsura" title="Nozu Michitsura">Nozu Michitsura</a><br /><a href="/wiki/%C5%8Cyama_Iwao" title="Ōyama Iwao">Ōyama Iwao</a><br /><a href="/wiki/It%C5%8D_Sukeyuki" title="Itō Sukeyuki">Itō Sukeyuki</a></td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="background-color:#C3D6EF;text-align:center;vertical-align:middle;font-size:110%;">Strength</th></tr><tr><td style="width:50%;border-right:1px dotted #aaa;">
630,000 men</td><td style="width:50%;padding-left:0.25em">
240,616 men</td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="background-color:#C3D6EF;text-align:center;vertical-align:middle;font-size:110%;">Casualties and losses</th></tr><tr><td style="width:50%;border-right:1px dotted #aaa;">
35,000 dead and wounded</td><td style="width:50%;padding-left:0.25em">

style="font-weight:normal;"><a href="/wiki/Simplified_Chinese_characters" title="Simplified Chinese characters">Simplified Chinese</a></th><td><span style="font-size: 1rem"><span lang="zh-Hans" title="Chinese language text">甲午战争</span></span></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><table class="collapsible collapsed" style="padding:0;border:none;margin:-3px;width:auto;min-width:100%;font-size:100%;clear:none;float:none;background-color:transparent"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold;font-size: 100%; text-align: left; background-color: #f9ffbc;">Transcriptions</th></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;background-color: #dcffc9;"><a href="/wiki/Standard_Chinese" title="Standard Chinese">Standard Mandarin</a></th></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="font-weight:normal;"><a href="/wiki/Hanyu_Pinyin" class="mw-redirect" title="Hanyu Pinyin">Hanyu Pinyin</a></th><td>Jiǎwǔ Zhànzhēng</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;background-color: #b0c4de;">Japan–Qing War</th></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="font-weight:normal;"><a href="/wiki/Kanji" title="Kanji">Kanji</a></th><td><span lang="ja" title="Japanese language text">日清戦争</span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="font-weight:normal;"><a href="/wiki/Ky%C5%ABjitai" title="Kyūjitai">Kyūjitai</a></th><td><span lang="ja" title="Japanese language text">日清戰爭</span></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" style="text-align:center"><table class="collapsible collapsed" style="padding:0;border:none;margin:-3px;width:auto;min-width:100%;font-size:100%;clear:none;float:none;background-color:transparent"><tbody><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-size:125%;font-weight:bold;font-size: 100%; text-align: left; background-color: #f9ffbc;">Transcriptions</th></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="font-weight:normal;"><a href="/wiki/Romanization_of_Japanese" title="Romanization of Japanese">Romanization</a></th><td>Nisshin sensō</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" style="text-align:center;background-color: #b0c4de;">Qing-Japan War</th></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="font-weight: normal;"><a href="/wiki/Hangul" title="Hangul">Hangul</a></th><td><div style="display:inline;font-size:1rem;"><span lang="ko-Hang" title="Korean language text">청일전쟁</span></div></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" style="font-weight: normal;"><a href="/wiki/Hanja" title="Hanja">Hanja</a></th><td><div style="display:inline;font-size:1rem;"><span lang="ko-Hani" title="Korean language text">淸日戰爭</span></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>The <b>First Sino-Japanese War</b> (25 July 1894&#160;– 17 April 1895), also known as the <b>Chino-Japanese War</b>, was fought between <a href="/wiki/Qing_dynasty" title="Qing dynasty">China</a> and <a href="/wiki/Empire_of_Japan" title="Empire of Japan">Japan</a> primarily over influence in <a href="/wiki/Joseon" title="Joseon">Korea</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> After more than six months of unbroken successes by Japanese land and naval forces and the loss of the port of <a href="/wiki/Weihai" title="Weihai">Weihaiwei</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Qing" class="mw-redirect" title="Qing">Qing</a> government <a href="/wiki/Suing_for_peace" title="Suing for peace">sued for peace</a> in February 1895.
</p><p>The war demonstrated the failure of the Qing dynasty's <a href="/wiki/Self-Strengthening_Movement" title="Self-Strengthening Movement">attempts to modernize its military</a> and fend off threats to its sovereignty, especially when compared with Japan's successful <a href="/wiki/Meiji_Restoration" title="Meiji Restoration">Meiji Restoration</a>. For the first time, regional dominance in <a href="/wiki/East_Asia" title="East Asia">East Asia</a> shifted from China to Japan;<sup id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEPaine20033_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEPaine20033-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> the prestige of the Qing Dynasty, along with the classical tradition in China, suffered a major blow. The humiliating loss of Korea as a <a href="/wiki/Tributary_state" title="Tributary state">tributary state</a> sparked an unprecedented public outcry. Within China, the defeat was a catalyst for a series of political upheavals led by <a href="/wiki/Sun_Yat-sen" title="Sun Yat-sen">Sun Yat-sen</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kang_Youwei" title="Kang Youwei">Kang Youwei</a>, culminating in the 1911 <a href="/wiki/Xinhai_Revolution" title="Xinhai Revolution">Xinhai Revolution</a>.
</p><p>The war is commonly known in China as the <b>War of Jiawu</b> (<a href="/wiki/Simplified_Chinese_characters" title="Simplified Chinese characters">Chinese</a>&#58; <span lang="zh-Hans">甲午戰爭</span>; <a href="/wiki/Pinyin" title="Pinyin">pinyin</a>&#58; <i><span lang="zh-Latn-pinyin">Jiǎwǔ Zhànzhēng</span></i>), referring to the year (1894) as named under the traditional <a href="/wiki/Sexagenary_cycle" title="Sexagenary cycle">sexagenary system</a> of years. In Japan, it is called the <b>Japan–Qing War</b><span style="font-weight: normal">&#32;(<a href="/wiki/Japanese_language" title="Japanese language">Japanese</a>:&#32;<span lang="ja">日清戦争</span><span style="display:none">,</span>&#32;<a href="/wiki/Hepburn_romanization" title="Hepburn romanization">Hepburn</a>:&#32;<i>Nisshin sensō</i>)</span>. In Korea, where much of the war took place, it is called the <b>Qing–Japan War</b> (<a href="/wiki/Korean_language" title="Korean language">Korean</a>: <span lang="ko">청일전쟁</span>; <a href="/wiki/Hanja" title="Hanja">Hanja</a>: 淸日戰爭).
</p>
